<user>116886803719605764106< /user>< user_name>
Jill Obermire< /user_name>
< time>
1532287951963</time>
<rate>2<//rate>< review>
Over the past 5 or so years, we've attended several Pump-it-Up parties at the Irvine location for our kids.  We also hosted a party for our daughter several years, and then yesterday had the opportunity to host a party for our son.

As a guest or coming to Pump-it-Up for open jump sessions, I would give this location a 4 star review.  Kids always have a great time, which is the main goal here, right?

My 2 star rating is based on our experience in hosting our son's birthday party yesterday.

For a weekend party with up to 25 kids, it costs $390, and this does not include the mandatory charges for pizza, drinks etc.  So, for a party to include your family, and kids from school, etc. we paid around $525.  (This doesn't include decorations, goodies bags, balloons, cake, etc.)  For our family, this is a large amount for a birthday party, therefore, I have high expectations.

Bottom line, I was disappointed with the staff that was assigned to our group yesterday.  They kept miscounting the number of children that were attending our party, they tangled up our birthday balloons, they did not follow-through with specific requests (but very simple requests) for the party set-up and how we wanted my son's birthday wish & cupcake-candle blow-out to go down.  They also forgot to turn-on the special light show and didn't follow-through with playing a game with the kids after pizza time.  Although our coordinator was sweet, I did give her specific directions that simply weren't followed.  I also felt like every time I tried to find her, I simply couldn't.

I was also expecting more help from Pump-It-Up staff for serving pizza, fruit and cupcakes.  Instead, we were just assigned 1 coordinator for our party.  It created stress for myself and my family having to handle so much in the party room, instead of being able to sit back and enjoy our friends and family that traveled to celebrate and enjoy our children.

Isn't that what we were paying for with having our party hosted there?

4 years ago, this was not the case when we hosted our daughter's birthday party here.

I'm disappointed and feel that I completely overpaid due to the lack of service support.  I really would recommend finding another venue to host your child's next birthday!< /review>

< text>
I had a birthday party for both of my kids at this place. It was so much fun. all the invited kids (ages 2-7) and their parents (include me) had a blast. One of their parents thanked me afterwards for how well her son napped that afternoon after the 10-12 party exhausted him pretty well. lol.
The best thing is that I don't have to spend time planning the party. All the little details are taken care of. The most time I spent on was deciding how many pizzas to get and what kind. BTW, the pizzas are actually pretty good. I wouldn't have been able to throw a party without Pump it up making it so easy for me. I was able to enjoy the party, have fun with the kids, instead of worrying about the logistics. The staff were all very friendly and professional. They did make a couple minor mistakes which didn't bother me personally, 1) they forgot to turn on the bubbles feature which I requested for one of the jump rooms; 2) they forgot to hang one of the banners I brought. But the rest of the party was perfect and without any hiccups.
In my opinion, the party price is very reasonable, but the food cost adds up, so bring as much as you are allowed to on your own.< /text>

<Review>My car suddenly started making loud noises, and then my check engine light came on, so I was concerned that it was something serious. Since it was right after Christmas I was also concerned about how much it would cost. I looked around online for someone locally and started reading the different reviews. They mentioned that this place was honest and did great work. When I got there, there were a few people ahead of me, and more kept showing up, it was also close to lunch time, so I was concerned that it would take long for my car to get checked and worked on. A few minutes later my car was lifted and looked at, and the manager Paul told me, that my issue was not serious, it was only the oxygen sensor that had come loose, and it would only cost $30 for them to have it fixed. It's true, the manager Paul is very honest! They could have made up a story and told me it was something more serious to charge me more, but he didn't. My car was quickly fixed, and sounds normal now. I can see why people take the time to write good reviews about this place. I'd highly recommend them!<//Review>< pictures>

< Review>
Since we live in Connecticut, every year I give my daughter (who lives in Hacienda Heights) a Christmas gift card for what I think looks to be an interesting restaurant.  Well I have never had a problem with charging it to my credit card (not a debit card), until today.  After much research I thought De Luca's would be a very nice place for my daughter and husband to have a wonderful Italian meal and the ambience looked quite lovely.  And, I thought that when we would visit we might go there for dinner sometime.

When a gentleman got on the phone he said that they didn't accept credit cards. Because he was sort of evasive in his explanation, I was made to think that this was because I was calling from out of state.  What that would have to do with anything when all I wanted to do was buy a $60 dollar Christmas gift card for their restaurant.  I have an excellent credit rating and have never had my credit card turned down even in Europe.  I was insulted.  He seemed to be hemming and hawing around the discussion.

As I have stated, I have done this with other restaurants in his vicinity and never had a problem.  In fact, they were very happy to accommodate my request and accepted my credit card with absolutely no hassle.   Sorry to say, when we visit we will not be stopping by this restaurant.<//Review>

First time at this restaurant. Had a white Coat Ceremony dinner for God Child in Optometry School. The food was divine. The vast menu has a dish for everyone. The food was prepared with fresh ingredients, hot and savory. The portions were large. We were able to enjoy the remaining food for a second meal. I had the chicken Marsala. So tender and the linguini sauce melted in your mouth. My husband had the lazagna prepared old school with fresh beef, thick cheese, hearty sauce and a hint of anised. He said it was the best  he ever had. My God daughter had the clam linguini. It looked moist, lots of pasta with light sauce. My God son had chicken parm. It too looked hearty. He said the meat was tender and there were two portions in one. The service was quick and very friendly. Lovely warm setting to celebrate a great event. Too stuffed to have desert.< /review>

Dr Rice never tried anything but to continue to reglue or cement it on. Finally Dr Amathyst took over and did her best but still no luck.  I used the rest of my insurance for the year for this procedure and made it clear that I wanted a refund for the one crown, so I could go to another dentist. Office staff agreed this was an understanble request especially considering how many times I've had to miss work just to come in and stated I would be issued a refund. It has been over two months that I asked for a refund, money that I paid out of pocket, and I continue to get lead around. Jay Hall</Name>
<Date>1492135281277</Date><Rating>1< /Rating>< text>
TFD, the Augustus name is simply a nickname given in university to me. Your rebuttal below assures me I made the right decision in finding another dentist.

For others in Turlock, my original review said this:

Because of unnecessary procedures done on me as a child, I have had dental problems throughout my adult life. This has made me very leery of dentists and it is very hard for me to know which dentists really wish the best for your health versus those who wish to do as many procedures possible so that they can enlarge their bottom line.
When I moved to Turlock about eight years ago, I needed to find a dentist locally that I could trust and decided to try Turlock Family Dentistry and Dr Jeffery Rice because a few other people told me that he was decent. So, I made an appointment and visited his office for a cleaning and initial inspection.
During that initial appointment, I was pushed to have a deep cleaning (the dental world calls this Root Planing and Scaling). Dr Jeffery Rice it turns out missed a small localized infection above one bicuspid. Perhaps it is just me, but I also found Dr Rice to be mildly enacius. During my second visit for a cleaning six months later, I was again pushed to have a deep cleaning. Beginning to grow suspicious, I went to two other dentists in Turlock and had second opinions. I found, I did not need a deep cleaning and that I had a small cavity that Dr Rice had missed.
Overall, I did not have the best experience with TFD. They have a dedicated business office attached to their practice and as soon as they figure out who you are and if you have a decent dental plan, they will begin telling you that you have "unused" dental coverage. And it seems, that if you fall into this group, then you will be mildly pestered by them for different types of procedures that may not be necessary (like deep cleanings). I am fortunate to have an excellent dental plan and every time I came, the office staff suggested I have either teeth whitening or deep cleanings.
Dr Rice also has wisely set up his entire practice so profits are maximized, because Dr Adamic, Dr Schellinck and others all work under one roof. At first this seems ideal because you never need to leave TFD to go to a specialist anywhere else. But the downside is that if you have a complaint, and that specialist is only there one day every two weeks then it can be difficult to settle a matter.
TFD is also at the high end of the market in what they charge for a specific procedure. Whether that be a cleaning, a cavity or a crown. I inquired for example with Dr Schellinck about getting a dental implant and the total cost for that molar position would have been about $5600. However, numerous other respected dentists in Turlock will do the same job for about $3200 to $4800, .... a major savings.
Picking a dentist is a personal decision and for me, I just came away feeling a little bit like Dr Rice is more interested in financing his next camper bus or his second home than he is in making sure I have great dental health. Your mileage may vary but never fear picking up a second or third opinion. I did, and I can highly recommend either Dr Antoine Varani or Dr Robert Mcculla in Turlock.<//text>
